src=3D'/images/drasks.png' alt=3D'Dr. Merrill Asks some important=\r\n questions of interest to Midtown East residents - Chiropractor Midtown Eas=\r\nt' border=3D'0' align=3D'absmiddle'> Dr. Merrill Asks...</h4><div id=3D\"ask=\r\n\" class=3D\"rounded\">=0D=0A\t\t<div class=3D'dhtmlgoodies_question'>Can someon=\r\ne who has had back surgery receive <strong>chiropractic</strong> care?</div=\r\n>=0D=0A\t\t<div class=3D'dhtmlgoodies_answer'><div>Yes. Rest assured that we =\r\nwill avoid the surgically modified areas of your spine. However, what we fi=\r\nnd is that surgical interventions will often produce spinal instability abo=\r\nve or below the involved level. This is will be the focus of your <strong>c=\r\nhiropractic</strong> care.</div></div>=0D=0A\t\t<div class=3D'dhtmlgoodies_qu=\r\nestion'>What's the difference between a \"good\" drug and a \"bad\" drug?</div>=\r\n=0D=0A\t\t<div class=3D'dhtmlgoodies_answer'><div>As a <strong>chiropractor</=\r\nstrong>, I see the use of many drugs (legal or illegal) as merely symptom t=\r\nreating. Worse, virtually every drug produces unwanted effects. The effects=\r\n of <strong>chiropractic</strong> are largely <em>positive </em>effects. If=\r\n you're a <strong>Midtown East</strong> parent, consider carefully before g=\r\niving your child a cough medication, cold remedy or pain reliever so this s=\r\nort of question doesn't arise in the first place.</div></div>=0D=0A\t</div><=\r\n/div>=0D=0A\t\t\t<div class=3D'banner'><a href=3D'/doctor/chiropractor/20S/chi=\r\nropractic-Midtown East/physiology.htm'><img src=3D'http://images.vortala.co=\r\nm/chiropractor/promotions/nervous_system.gif' border=3D'0'  alt=3D'Your ner=\r\nvous system controls everything' ></a></div>=0D=0A=0D=0A\t\t\t\t</div>=0D=0A\t\t\t=\r\n</div>\t\t\t\t<h3>Spinal Fusion: Just the Facts</h3><img class=3D\"imgcaption fl=\r\noatr\" title=3D\"Before you go under the knife, be sure you understand the ri=\r\nsks of spinal fusion surgery.\" alt=3D\"Backaches and sciatica image.\" src=3D=\r\n\"http://images.vortala.com/chiropractor/graphics/da_topical/apr10/spinal_fu=\r\nsion.jpg\">=0A<p>Most people have at least one episode of low back pain at s=\r\nome point in their lives. And many, in fact, experience chronic low back pa=\r\nin. </p>=0A<p>When traditional medical treatments, such as physical therapy=\r\n, exercise and medication fail to bring about any long-lasting relief, a do=\r\nctor may recommend spinal fusion surgery to correct the problem. This usual=\r\nly occurs in situations where there is degenerative disc disease, a herniat=\r\ned disc or a severe injury to the spine. Spinal fusion surgery is sometimes=\r\n recommended to correct scoliosis (curvature of the spine) or other irregul=\r\nar curves in the spine. </p>=0A<p>What happens during fusion surgery? In a =\r\n2 - 12 hour long procedure, under general anesthesia, bone from the patient=\r\n's hip, or from a donor, is used to graft two adjacent vertebrae. The graft=\r\n is put in place so that the disc and joints between them are no longer abl=\r\ne to move. The fusion forms a bridge, using bone, screws, rods and pins tha=\r\nt link the vertebrae together. This provides stability to the spine and red=\r\nuces pain. At least that's the intent of the surgery. </p>=0A<p>Risks invol=\r\nved? There are several: administration of general anesthesia, bleeding, inf=\r\nection, rejection of donor bone, blood clots, stroke, heart attack and nerv=\r\ne damage. Full recovery can take up to a year or even longer. The success r=\r\nate may actually be lower in patients with diabetes and osteoporosis, those=\r\n who smoke or are overweight, and those who may have had radiation therapy =\r\nthat included the lower spine. </p>=0A<p>Obviously there are risks with any=\r\n surgery, but back surgery patients frequently suffer from Failed Back Surg=\r\nery Syndrome. This occurs when a patient is in the same or worse shape as t=\r\nhey were in <em>prior</em> to the surgery. </p>=0A<p>Chiropractic care has =\r\nshown some impressive results in patients with scoliosis, degenerative disc=\r\n disease or herniated discs. Many patients have avoided surgery altogether =\r\nafter undergoing routine chiropractic care. We believe that it is an altern=\r\native that deserves careful consideration when other traditional approaches=\r\n to back pain have been tried and have failed. Chiropractic adjustments, al=\r\nong with other non-invasive treatment modalities, may make surgery an optio=\r\nn that doesn't even require consideration. </p>=0A<p><a href=3D\"/doctor/chi=\r\nropractor/209S/chiropractor-Midtown East/backaches-and-sciatica.htm\"><img s=\r\nrc=3D\"http://images.vortala.com/chiropractor/graphics/da_topical/Buttons/ba=\r\nckache.jpg\" The goal is to obtain the desired results in as little t=\r\nime as possible, at the lowest cost, and with the least amount of pain and =\r\ndowntime. </p>=0D=0A<p>And=85usually, patients have an exact picture in the=\r\nir head of what they want, and expect to see when the procedure is done, us=\r\nually with the help of the surgeon=92s software that can reconstruct the ap=\r\nplicable area on a computer screen. Or maybe he =\r\nor she is suddenly afraid of the dark or is starting to experience night te=\r\nrrors =96 these can be very frightening experiences for parents. </p>=0D=0A=\r\n<p>Rest assured=85you are not alone; most toddlers experience night fears a=\r\nt some point and you are in the perfect position to help your child to get =\r\nover them.</p>=0D=0A<p>Here are several suggestions that might help:</p>=0D=\r\n=0A<p>&#8226; Monitor your child=92s television viewing. Fires, shootings, robberies, and dea=\r\nths can have a huge effect on a young child who doesn=92t understand and wh=\r\no doesn=92t have the language skills to communicate his or her fears. Even =\r\ncartoons show some scary-looking characters!</p>=0D=0A<p>&#8226; Don=92t ar=\r\ngue with your spouse in front of your child. This amount of light is reassuring and it isn=92t enough t=\r\no keep your child from falling asleep.</p>=0D=0A<p>&#8226; Sit with your ch=\r\nild for a few minutes and reassure him or her that everything is fine and t=\r\nhat you are close by to protect him or her.</p>=0D=0A<p>&#8226; Establish a=\r\n regular bedtime routine and stick to it as much as possible (ex., bath, pr=\r\nayers, bedtime story, lullaby and a hug and kiss goodnight).</p>=0D=0A<p>&#=\r\n8226; Encourage your child to draw pictures or to talk about what he or she=\r\n sees in the dark. And while the complex chemical and electrical nature of this vast netw=\r\nork is best left to others, here are four key things you should know:</p><i=\r\nmg class=3D\"imgcaption floatr\" title=3D\"When the neurological circuits have=\r\n integrity, your body works as it was designed.\" alt=3D\"Safety pin closed\" =\r\nsrc=3D\"http://images.vortala.com/chiropractor/graphics/AUS_Parent_Images/sa=\r\nfety_pin_closed.jpg\" /> <img class=3D\"imgcaption\" title=3D\"When spinal vert=\r\nebrae pinch or choke nerves, affected organs and tissues don=92t work the w=\r\nay they should and ill-health results. \" alt=3D\"Safety pin open\" src=3D\"htt=\r\np://images.vortala.com/chiropractor/graphics/AUS_Parent_Images/safety_pin_o=\r\npen.jpg\" /> =0D=0A<h5>Efferent Communications</h5>=0D=0A<p>Nerve impulses a=\r\nre sent from the brain out to the organs and tissues of your body.</p>=0D=\r\n=0A<h5>Afferent Communications</h5>=0D=0A<p>Nerve impulses are sent back to=\r\n the brain to make sure everything is working correctly.</p>=0D=0A<h5>Compr=\r\nessive Lesions</h5>=0D=0A<p>If spinal vertebrae pinch or choke nerve tissue=\r\n, signals going from or to the affected organ or tissue can be diminished. =\r\n(i.e., constipation.)</p>=0D=0A<h5>Facilitative Lesions</h5>=0D=0A<p>If spi=\r\nnal vertebrae chafe or irritate nerve tissue, signals going from or to the =\r\naffected organ or tissue can be excited. (i.e., diarrhea.)</p>=0D=0A<p>The =\r\nnervous system is vulnerable where delicate nerve tissue comes into proximi=\r\nty with the moving bones of your spine.
